### Component Summary: JVZ14N391K87PU5 (Metal Oxide Varistor)

#### Key Specifications:
- **Voltage Ratings:**
  - Varistor Voltage: 390V (at 1mA)
  - Maximum Allowable Voltage: 450V (DC)
  - Maximum Clamping Voltage: 650V (at 8/20µs)
  
- **Current Ratings:**
  - Withstanding Surge Current: 20kA (8/20µs)
  - Nominal Discharge Current: 1kA (8/20µs)

- **Power Consumption:**
  - Rated Wattage: 40W
  - Energy (10/1000µs): 50J

- **Operating Temperature Range:**
  - -40°C to +125°C

- **Package Type:**
  - Disc type, Ø14mm

- **Special Features:**
  - High surge capability
  - Suitable for transient voltage suppression
  - Moisture Sensitive Level: MSL 1 (JEDEC J-STD-020E)

#### Description:
The JVZ14N391K87PU5 is a Metal Oxide Varistor (MOV) designed to protect electronic circuits from voltage spikes and transients. It operates by exhibiting high resistance under normal conditions and low resistance during voltage surges, effectively clamping excess voltage and preventing damage to sensitive components.

#### Typical Applications:
- **Surge Protection:** Commonly used in power supply circuits, telecommunications, and consumer electronics to protect against voltage spikes caused by lightning, switching operations, or other transient events.
- **Power Management:** Helps in maintaining voltage levels within safe limits, ensuring the reliability and longevity of electronic devices.
- **Signal Line Protection:** Used in data lines and communication interfaces to safeguard against overvoltage conditions.

This varistor is particularly suitable for applications requiring robust surge protection and is compliant with various international safety and performance standards.
